ISNULL((select SUM(VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_InvoiceAmountExVAT - CASE WHEN VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_DetType = 2 THEN 0.0 ELSE VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_NetCostTotalLocalNoVat END)
from VRD_OutOrderDet  with(index(IX_VRD_ID_OutOrder))
inner join VRD_OutOrder  on VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_OutOrder = VRD_OutOrder.ID
INNER JOIN VRD_B_PayMethod pm ON VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_B_PayMethod = VRD_B_PayMethod.ID
where VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_OutInvoice IS NOT NULL
AND VRD_OutOrder.VRD_ID_CarSale = VRD_CarSale.ID
AND VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_PayType = 1 AND VRD_B_PayMethod.VRD_BMTCarsExtraGear = 0), 0.0)
ISNULL((
SELECT SUM(ccad.VRD_CommissionAmountFact)
FROM VRD_CreditContract cc
INNER JOIN VRD_CreditConActDet ccad ON cc.ID = ccad.VRD_ID_CreditContract
INNER JOIN VRD_CreditConAct cca ON cca.ID = ccad.VRD_ID_CreditConAct
WHERE cc.VRD_ID_CarSale = VRD_CarSale.ID and cca.VRD_Status not in (4)
), 0.0)
ISNULL((
SELECT SUM(iad.VRD_CommissionAmountFact)
FROM VRD_InsuranceActDet iad
INNER JOIN VRD_InsuranceAct ia ON iad.VRD_ID_InsuranceAct = ia.ID
INNER JOIN VRD_InsuranceContract ic ON iad.VRD_ID_InsuranceContract = ic.ID
WHERE ic.VRD_ID_CarSale = VRD_CarSale.ID AND ia.VRD_Status not in (4)
), 0.0)
ISNULL((select SUM(VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_InvoiceAmountExVAT - CASE WHEN VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_DetType = 2 THEN 0.0 ELSE VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_NetCostTotalLocalNoVat END)
from VRD_OutOrderDet  with(index(IX_VRD_ID_OutOrder))
inner join VRD_OutOrder  on VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_OutOrder = VRD_OutOrder.ID
INNER JOIN VRD_B_PayMethod pm ON VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_B_PayMethod = VRD_B_PayMethod.ID
where VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_OutInvoice IS NOT NULL
AND (VRD_OutOrder.VRD_ID_CarSale = VRD_CarSale.ID OR VRD_OutOrder.VRD_ID_CarOrder = VRD_CarSale.VRD_ID_CarOrder OR VRD_OutOrder.VRD_ID_UsedCar = VRD_CarSale.VRD_ID_UsedCar)
AND VRD_B_PayMethod.VRD_BMTCarsExtraGear = 1), 0.0)

SELECT SUM(csd.VRD_AmountLocalExVAT - ISNULL(csd.VRD_NetCostLocalCalcNoVat, 0.0)) FROM VRD_CarSaleDetail csd
inner join VRD_CarSale  on csd.VRD_ID_CarSale = VRD_CarSale.ID
inner join VRD_UsedCar  on VRD_CarSale.VRD_ID_UsedCar = VRD_UsedCar.ID

ISNULL((SELECT SUM(CASE WHEN VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_DetType in (3,4) THEN VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_NetCostTotalLocalNoVat ELSE 0.0 END)
FROM VRD_OutOrderDet ood with (index(IX_VRD_ID_OutOrder))

inner join VRD_B_PayMethod  ON VRD_OutOrderDet.VRD_ID_B_PayMethod = VRD_B_PayMethod.ID

AND VRD_B_PayMethod.VRD_BMTCarsPriceAdding = 0
), 0.0)
